</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC113" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="113" style="position:relative"><span class="pl-mh">reveal<span class="pl-k">~</span></span></div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC114" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="114" style="position:relative">This is a boolean flag. </div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC117" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="117" style="position:relative"><span class="pl-mh">reveal_file<span class="pl-k">~</span></span></div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC118" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="118" style="position:relative">A path to a file to reveal. </div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC124" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="124" style="position:relative"><span class="pl-mh">reveal_force_cwd<span class="pl-k">~</span></span></div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC125" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="125" style="position:relative">This is a boolean flag. </div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC131" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="131" style="position:relative"><span class="pl-mh">selector<span class="pl-k">~</span></span></div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC132" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="132" style="position:relative">This is a boolean flag. </div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC749" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="749" style="position:relative">By adding or replacing <span class="pl-ms">|</span><span class="pl-c1">neo-tree-components</span><span class="pl-ms">|</span>. Components are the functions</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC750" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="750" style="position:relative">called by the renderers, and they return the text and highlight group to be</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC751" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="751" style="position:relative">displayed.  : all merged to the right            /  ~  \  ~  \  ~  \...</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC896" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="896" style="position:relative">    &#039;&quot;left&quot;&#039;   : all merged to the left             /  ~  /  ~  /  ~  /...</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC897" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="897" style="position:relative">    &#039;&quot;active&quot;&#039; : merged towards the active tab      /  ~  / focused tab \  ~  \...</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC898" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="898" style="position:relative">When set to string such as &quot;┃&quot;, it is equivalent to</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC899" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="899" style="position:relative">`{ left = &quot;┃&quot;, right = &quot;┃&quot;, override = &quot;active&quot; }`.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC900" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="900" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC901" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="901" style="position:relative"><span class="pl-c1">`show_separator_on_edge`</span> takes a boolean value where <span class="pl-c1">`false`</span> (default) hides the</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC902" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="902" style="position:relative">separators on the far left / right. </div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC908" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="908" style="position:relative">CURRENT WORKING DIRECTORY                                         <span class="pl-k">*neo-tree-cwd*</span></div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC909" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="909" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC910" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="910" style="position:relative">By default, Neo-tree will maintain a two-way binding between the cwd of nvim and</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC911" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="911" style="position:relative">the root of the tree. Changing the root in Neo-tree will change the working</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC912" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="912" style="position:relative">directory of nvim and vice versa.</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC913" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="913" style="position:relative">
</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC914" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="914" style="position:relative">In the case of a sidebar, this will be synced with the tab working directory</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC915" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="915" style="position:relative">(<span class="pl-ms">|</span><span class="pl-c1">tcd</span><span class="pl-ms">|</span>). </div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC918" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="918" style="position:relative">These defaults can be changed by setting the following options:</div></div></div><div class="react-code-text react-code-line-contents" style="min-height:auto"><div><div id="LC919" class="react-file-line html-div" data-testid="code-cell" data-line-number="919" style="position:relative">
